<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="autocomplete" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#autocomplete"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Autocomplete</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoComplete</code> prop to manage autocompletion in the input.</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">new-password</code> — The user is creating a new password.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">current-password</code> — The user is entering an existing password.</li>
</ul>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8jhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8jhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8jhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled-visibility" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled-visibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled Visibility</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">visible</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onVisibilityChange</code> props to control the visibility of the password input.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the password input is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">usePasswordInput</code> hook.
This way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s an example of how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">PasswordInput</code> component with the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="password-managers" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#password-managers"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Password Managers</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ignorePasswordManager</code> prop to ignore password managers like 1Password, LastPass, etc. This is useful for
non-login scenarios (e.g., &quot;api keys&quot;, &quot;secure notes&quot;, &quot;temporary passwords&quot;)</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Currently, this only works for 1Password, LastPass, Bitwarden, Dashlane, and Proton Pass.</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="strength-meter" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#strength-meter"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Strength Meter</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Combine the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">PasswordInput</code> with a password strength library to show visual feedback about password strength. This
example uses the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/check-password-strength" class="link"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">check-password-strength</code></a> package to provide
real-time strength validation.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="validation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#validation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Validation</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Combine with custom validation logic to show real-time feedback. Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">invalid</code> prop to indicate validation errors.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

creating a new password.\n- `current-password` — The user is entering an existing password.\n\n**Example: autocomplete**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Autocomplete = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Root className={styles.Root} autoComplete=\"new-password\"\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger className={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n          \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled Visibility\n\nUse the `visible` and `onVisibilityChange` props to control the visibility of the password input.\n\n**Example: controlled-visibility**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledVisibility = () =\u003e {\n  const [visible, setVisible] = useState(false)\n  return (\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Root className={styles.Root} visible={visible} onVisibilityChange={(e) =\u003e setVisible(e.visible)}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003ePassword is {visible ? 'visible' : 'hidden'}\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger className={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledVisibility = () =\u003e {\n  const [visible, setVisible] = createSignal(false)\n  return (\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Root class={styles.Root} visible={visible()} onVisibilityChange={(e) =\u003e setVisible(e.visible)}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003ePassword is {visible() ? 'visible' : 'hidden'}\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger class={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nconst visible = ref(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model:visible=\"visible\"\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003ePassword is {{ visible ? 'visible' : 'hidden' }}\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger :class=\"styles.VisibilityTrigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #fallback\u003e\n            \u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/password-input'\n  import { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\n  let visible = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPasswordInput.Root class={styles.Root} bind:visible\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003e\n    Password is {visible ? 'visible' : 'hidden'}\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger class={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        {#snippet fallback()}\n          \u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n        \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the password input is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `usePasswordInput` hook.\nThis way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput, usePasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const passwordInput = usePasswordInput()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003epassword input is {passwordInput.visible ? 'visible' : 'hidden'}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={passwordInput}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger className={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput, usePasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const passwordInput = usePasswordInput()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003epassword input is {passwordInput().visible ? 'visible' : 'hidden'}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={passwordInput}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger class={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PasswordInput, usePasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nconst passwordInput = usePasswordInput()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003epassword input is {{ passwordInput.visible ? \u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e\n          {/snippet}\n          \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n component.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger managers like 1Password, LastPass, etc. This is useful for\nnon-login scenarios (e.g., \"api keys\", \"secure notes\", \"temporary passwords\")\n\n\u003e **Currently, this only works for 1Password, LastPass, Bitwarden, Dashlane, and Proton Pass.**\n\n**Example: ignore-password-manager**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const IgnorePasswordManager = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Root className={styles.Root} ignorePasswordManagers\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eAPI Key\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Input className={styles.Input} defaultValue=\"spd_1234567890\" /\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger className={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n          \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from    \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #fallback\u003e\n            \u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n strength. This\nexample uses the [`check-password-strength`](https://www.npmjs.com/package/check-password-strength) package to provide\nreal-time strength validation.\n\n**Example: strength-meter**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { passwordStrength, type Options } from 'check-password-strength'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useMemo, useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nconst strengthOptions: Options\u003cstring\u003e = [\n  { id: 0, value: 'weak', minDiversity: 0, minLength: 0 },\n  { id: 1, value: 'medium', minDiversity: 2, minLength: 6 },\n  { id: 2, value: 'strong', minDiversity: 4, minLength: 8 },\n]\n\nexport const StrengthMeter = () =\u003e {\n  const [password, setPassword] = useState('asdfasdf')\n\n  const strength = useMemo(() =\u003e {\n    if (!password) return null\n    const { value } = passwordStrength(password, strengthOptions)\n    return value\n  }, [password])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Input\n          className={styles.Input}\n          value={password}\n          onChange={(e) =\u003e setPassword(e.currentTarget.value)}\n          placeholder=\"Enter your password\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger className={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n      {strength \u0026\u0026 (\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.StrengthMeter}\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.StrengthBar}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.StrengthFill} data-strength={strength} /\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.StrengthLabel}\u003e{strength} password\u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/password-input'\nimport { passwordStrength, type Options } from 'check-password-strength'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createMemo, createSignal, Show } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nconst strengthOptions: Options\u003cstring\u003e = [\n  { id: 0, value: 'weak', minDiversity: 0, minLength: 0 },\n  { id: 1, value: 'medium', minDiversity: 2, minLength: 6 },\n  { id: 2, value: 'strong', minDiversity: 4, minLength: 8 },\n]\n\nexport const StrengthMeter = () =\u003e {\n  const [password, setPassword] = createSignal('asdfasdf')\n\n  const strength = createMemo(() =\u003e {\n    if (!password()) return null\n    const { value } = passwordStrength(password(), strengthOptions)\n    return value\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Input\n          class={styles.Input}\n          value={password()}\n          onInput={(e) =\u003e setPassword(e.currentTarget.value)}\n          placeholder=\"Enter your password\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger class={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003cShow when={strength()}\u003e\n        {(value) =\u003e (\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthMeter}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthBar}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthFill} data-strength={value()} /\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthLabel}\u003e{value()} password\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Show\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/password-input'\nimport { passwordStrength, type Options } from 'check-password-strength'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { computed, ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nconst strengthOptions: Options\u003cstring\u003e = [\n  { id: 0, value: 'weak', minDiversity: 0, minLength: 0 },\n  { id: 1, value: 'medium', minDiversity: 2, minLength: 6 },\n  { id: 2, value: 'strong', minDiversity: 4, minLength: 8 },\n]\n\nconst password = ref('asdfasdf')\n\nconst strength = computed(() =\u003e {\n  if (!password.value) return null\n  const { value } = passwordStrength(password.value, strengthOptions)\n  return value\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" v-model=\"password\" placeholder=\"Enter your password\" /\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger :class=\"styles.VisibilityTrigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #fallback\u003e\n            \u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003cdiv v-if=\"strength\" :class=\"styles.StrengthMeter\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.StrengthBar\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.StrengthFill\" :data-strength=\"strength\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.StrengthLabel\"\u003e{{ strength }} password\u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/password-input'\n  import { passwordStrength, type Options } from 'check-password-strength'\n  import { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\n  const strengthOptions: Options\u003cstring\u003e = [\n    { id: 0, value: 'weak', minDiversity: 0, minLength: 0 },\n    { id: 1, value: 'medium', minDiversity: 2, minLength: 6 },\n    { id: 2, value: 'strong', minDiversity: 4, minLength: 8 },\n  ]\n\n  let password = $state('asdfasdf')\n\n  const strength = $derived.by(() =\u003e {\n    if (!password) return null\n    const { value } = passwordStrength(password, strengthOptions)\n    return value\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cPasswordInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003ePassword\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Input class={styles.Input} bind:value={password} placeholder=\"Enter your password\" /\u003e\n    \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger class={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        {#snippet fallback()}\n          \u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n        \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n  \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n  {#if strength}\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthMeter}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthBar}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthFill} data-strength={strength}\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.StrengthLabel}\u003e{strength} password\u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  {/if}\n\u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Validation\n\nCombine with custom validation logic to show real-time feedback. Use the `invalid` prop to indicate validation errors.\n\n**Example: with-validation**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/react/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useMemo, useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nexport const WithValidation = () =\u003e {\n  const [password, setPassword] = useState('')\n  const isValid = useMemo(() =\u003e password.length \u003e= 8, [password])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cPasswordInput.Root className={styles.Root} invalid={!isValid \u0026\u0026 password.length \u003e 0}\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003ePassword (min 8 characters)\u003c/PasswordInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cPasswordInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.Input\n          className={styles.Input}\n          value={password}\n          onChange={(e) =\u003e setPassword(e.target.value)}\n          placeholder=\"Enter your password\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cPasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger className={styles.VisibilityTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cPasswordInput.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} fallback={\u003cEyeOffIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cEyeIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n      {password.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 !isValid \u0026\u0026 (\n        \u003cp className={styles.ValidationMessage} data-valid=\"false\"\u003e\n          Password must be at least 8 characters\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      )}\n      {isValid \u0026\u0026 password.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 (\n        \u003cp className={styles.ValidationMessage} data-valid=\"true\"\u003e\n          Password is valid\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createMemo, createSignal } from \u003c/PasswordInput.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/PasswordInput.VisibilityTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/PasswordInput.Control\u003e\n      {password().length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 !isValid() \u0026\u0026 password().length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 (\n        \u003cp class={styles.ValidationMessage} data-valid=\"true\"\u003e\n          Password is valid\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/PasswordInput.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { PasswordInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/password-input'\nimport { EyeIcon, EyeOffIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { computed, ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/password-input.module.css'\n\nconst password = ref('')\nconst isValid = computed(() =\u003e password.value.length \u003e= 8)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cPasswordInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :invalid=\"!isValid \u0026\u0026 password.length \u003e 0\"\u003e\n
